function
changePos()
{ width = document.body.clientWidth; height = document.body.clientHeight; Hoffset = img.offsetHeight; Woffset = img.offsetWidth; img.style.left = xPos + document.body.scrollLeft; img.style.top = yPos + document.body.scrollTop; if (yon) { yPos = yPos + step; } else { yPos = yPos - step; } if (yPos < 0) { yon = 1; yPos = 0; } if (yPos >= (height - Hoffset)) { yon = 0; yPos = (height - Hoffset); } if (xon) { xPos = xPos + step; } else { xPos = xPos - step; } if (xPos < 0) { xon = 1; xPos = 0; } if (xPos >= (width - Woffset)) { xon = 0; xPos = (width - Woffset); } }
